             <div class="main section" id="main">
              <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Monday, January 13, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-J1zNTvXqsRo/UtNbilUVfQI/AAAAAAAAXt0/fx7eGqF3kD8/s72-c/wood+quilt+1.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="772980434779300135" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="120880747083540509" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="120880747083540509">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     "W" is for Wood Planked Quilt
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-120880747083540509" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Build: diy wood planked quilt wall art
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-J1zNTvXqsRo/UtNbilUVfQI/AAAAAAAAXt0/fx7eGqF3kD8/s1600/wood+quilt+1.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-J1zNTvXqsRo/UtNbilUVfQI/AAAAAAAAXt0/fx7eGqF3kD8/s1600/wood+quilt+1.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Make this wall decor using pine boards, glue and various stains.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      It makes a great statement and combines two of my favorites: wood and sewing!
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FOzE_KDXZYc/UtNbjLMmcuI/AAAAAAAAXuY/SDfvV4-w_4M/s1600/wood+quilt+3.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-FOzE_KDXZYc/UtNbjLMmcuI/AAAAAAAAXuY/SDfvV4-w_4M/s1600/wood+quilt+3.jpg" width="425"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <a name="more">
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oFPI38WZd48/UtNbkSJi80I/AAAAAAAAXug/mJWygOWYOvM/s1600/wood+quilt+6.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oFPI38WZd48/UtNbkSJi80I/AAAAAAAAXug/mJWygOWYOvM/s1600/wood+quilt+6.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Inspired by
                      <a href="http://www.potterybarn.com/products/planked-wood-quilt-square-wall-art/" target="_blank">
                       Pottery Barn's planked quilt square
                      </a>
                      :
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-54yMwd5Ddb0/UtNcdDmNlhI/AAAAAAAAXu8/QTWi6WDInqQ/s1600/img77c.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="287" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-54yMwd5Ddb0/UtNcdDmNlhI/AAAAAAAAXu8/QTWi6WDInqQ/s1600/img77c.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://www.potterybarn.com/products/planked-wood-quilt-square-wall-art/" target="_blank">
                       <i>
                        <span style="font-size: x-small;">
                         image source
                        </span>
                       </i>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Their version will set you back $349 plus shipping.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      I made this diy version for $60.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BdistIakzPQ/UtNbkg6ijrI/AAAAAAAAXuc/ieYqe60bV_Y/s1600/wood+quilt+7.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-BdistIakzPQ/UtNbkg6ijrI/AAAAAAAAXuc/ieYqe60bV_Y/s1600/wood+quilt+7.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Even better I was able to tailor the stain colors to my liking.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      (The walls are painted Benjamin Moore sea pearl.)
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      The finished size of my version is 43.5" square.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZbTHN7Q5TzY/UtNbi59jJeI/AAAAAAAAXuM/HsdzNmRpczo/s1600/wood+quilt+2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ZbTHN7Q5TzY/UtNbi59jJeI/AAAAAAAAXuM/HsdzNmRpczo/s1600/wood+quilt+2.jpg" width="426"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2SvtWGFBOF8/UtNbmhw3OII/AAAAAAAAXu4/9EjjfFJq2Yg/s1600/wood+quilt+5.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2SvtWGFBOF8/UtNbmhw3OII/AAAAAAAAXu4/9EjjfFJq2Yg/s1600/wood+quilt+5.jpg" width="266"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      We've come a long way in
                      <a href="http://thatsmyletter.blogspot.com/2013/09/f-is-for-family-room-makeover.html" target="_blank">
                       the family room
                      </a>
                      in the past 6 months:
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-b0xi54T_LA0/UtNblvg82II/AAAAAAAAXus/FT36q09uEks/s1600/wood+quilt.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-b0xi54T_LA0/UtNblvg82II/AAAAAAAAXus/FT36q09uEks/s1600/wood+quilt.jpg"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <u>
                       How to build a wood planked quilt:
                      </u>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      1. Lumber:
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      6 - 1 x 4 x 8 pine boards
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      2 - 1 x 2 x 8 pine boards
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      1/2" plywood panel 4' x 4'
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      2. Make your cuts using the measurements below.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Cut one of each size and then use that piece as your guide to make the remaining cuts.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PyMbysZH-q0/UtNblJ8iAGI/AAAAAAAAXu0/EuwTYnYcWfQ/s1600/wood+quilt+cuts.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="284" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-PyMbysZH-q0/UtNblJ8iAGI/AAAAAAAAXu0/EuwTYnYcWfQ/s1600/wood+quilt+cuts.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      3.5" square x 4
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <u>
                       45 degree mitered cuts:
                      </u>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      7" at long end x 8
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      10.5" at long end x 8
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      4" at long end x 8
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      7.5" at long end x 8
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      11" at long end x 8
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      14.75" long to short x 16
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      3. Layout one corner square to determine final size.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Trim 1/2" plywood back piece to fit entire quilt.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Mine measured 20 3/4" so I cut my plywood at 41.5" x 41.5"
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      4. Stain all the pieces in multiple colors.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      I stacked the pieces in 4 groups (one for each square) then flipped 2 stacks over to be sure I would be staining the correct side.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hhUkvEFqtEU/UtNhquRCuRI/AAAAAAAAXvQ/_e2bC32ooQo/s1600/IMG_1759.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="244" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-hhUkvEFqtEU/UtNhquRCuRI/AAAAAAAAXvQ/_e2bC32ooQo/s1600/IMG_1759.JPG" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a6-QVvDoHOk/UtNhuRBr41I/AAAAAAAAXvg/cui4wb1fZr8/s1600/IMG_1762.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="221" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-a6-QVvDoHOk/UtNhuRBr41I/AAAAAAAAXvg/cui4wb1fZr8/s1600/IMG_1762.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      5. Begin placing the pieces on the plywood:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HkI4cxYFB-M/UtNhuzQzyzI/AAAAAAAAXvw/u9_WvlPPXT4/s1600/IMG_1763.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-HkI4cxYFB-M/UtNhuzQzyzI/AAAAAAAAXvw/u9_WvlPPXT4/s1600/IMG_1763.jpg" width="302"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      6. Mark the center point of the board to give you a guideline:
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-A-S2g_z6pZI/UtNhuh2FcFI/AAAAAAAAXvs/jMsqEk2JJU4/s1600/IMG_1764.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-A-S2g_z6pZI/UtNhuh2FcFI/AAAAAAAAXvs/jMsqEk2JJU4/s1600/IMG_1764.jpg" width="240"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      7. Once you are satisfied with the layout start gluing the pieces to the board.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      Any wood glue will work.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DbtRa4pyj1w/UtNhvEcVk9I/AAAAAAAAXv0/HYOOD-BySTM/s1600/IMG_1765.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="240" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DbtRa4pyj1w/UtNhvEcVk9I/AAAAAAAAXv0/HYOOD-BySTM/s1600/IMG_1765.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      8. Weigh down the pieces to dry:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vODzH42IT1g/UtNhvnhG8DI/AAAAAAAAXv8/sg1KrhZKTG0/s1600/IMG_1769.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="289" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vODzH42IT1g/UtNhvnhG8DI/AAAAAAAAXv8/sg1KrhZKTG0/s1600/IMG_1769.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      9. Before adding the trim frame check to be sure no boards are hanging long off the edge:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CYmphBbH7x8/UtNjPhfJwyI/AAAAAAAAXwY/TQnajP3UTGs/s1600/IMG_1770.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CYmphBbH7x8/UtNjPhfJwyI/AAAAAAAAXwY/TQnajP3UTGs/s1600/IMG_1770.jpg" width="240"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      10. Mark the long board with tape which gives you a cut line and protects the finish from and scratching by the jigsaw:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-okGjrFFq6Tc/UtNhwL8lSeI/AAAAAAAAXwA/0kVfyKNWTTw/s1600/IMG_1771.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-okGjrFFq6Tc/UtNhwL8lSeI/AAAAAAAAXwA/0kVfyKNWTTw/s1600/IMG_1771.jpg" width="240"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      11. Cut off the excess edge with a jig saw:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kxr_M6PZWbs/UtNjtX1pOtI/AAAAAAAAXwg/C64MgU0fmJM/s1600/IMG_1772.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kxr_M6PZWbs/UtNjtX1pOtI/AAAAAAAAXwg/C64MgU0fmJM/s1600/IMG_1772.jpg" width="240"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      12. Cut 1 x 2 boards to frame out edge. Glue and nail in place.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      13. Secure cleat to backside of plywood:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HjuPkLPP7AM/UtNhxJ4azEI/AAAAAAAAXwM/4c3nzyICxS0/s1600/IMG_1773.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="240" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HjuPkLPP7AM/UtNhxJ4azEI/AAAAAAAAXwM/4c3nzyICxS0/s1600/IMG_1773.JPG" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      14. Attach wall portion of cleat:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b0B5XALvTpQ/UtNhyKw2_AI/AAAAAAAAXwQ/J_EKQxPPb1o/s1600/IMG_1774.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="239" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-b0B5XALvTpQ/UtNhyKw2_AI/AAAAAAAAXwQ/J_EKQxPPb1o/s1600/IMG_1774.JPG" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      Hang and enjoy!
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, FreeMono, monospace; font-size: 13px; line-height: 18px;">
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, FreeMono, monospace; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; text-align: center;">
                      <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;">
                       I'm linking up to:
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, FreeMono, monospace; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, FreeMono, monospace; font-size: 13px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px; text-align: center;">

                       <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;">
                        <span class="Apple-style-span" style="line-height: 18px;">

                   I build, paint and sew everything sharing my tutorials here. It's all DIY all the time.

                    <script type="text/javascript">
                     window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes &amp;&amp; gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d772980434779300135\x26origin\x3dhttp://thatsmyletter.blogspot.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBjIyMjIyMiIGMjFiYjUzKgZmZmZmZmYyBjAwMDAwMDoGMjIyMjIyQgYyMWJiNTNKBjk5OTk5OVIGMjFiYjUzWgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d120880747083540509");
              },
              'open': function(url) {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen(url);
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
    }
    followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d772980434779300135\x26origin\x3dhttp://thatsmyletter.blogspot.com/\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaBjIyMjIyMiIGMjFiYjUzKgZmZmZmZmYyBjAwMDAwMDoGMjIyMjIyQgYyMWJiNTNKBjk5OTk5OVIGMjFiYjUzWgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudA%3D%3D\x26postID\x3d120880747083540509");
